âš™ï¸ STEP 2: CREATE plot_emoji_heatmap() FUNCTION
Create a new file called symbolic_ai/emoji_heatmap.py:
python
CopyEdit
# symbolic_ai/emoji_heatmap.py

import pandas as pd
import plotly.express as px
from symbolic_ai.emotion_mapper import emoji_map

def plot_emoji_heatmap():
    df = pd.DataFrame(emoji_map)

    fig = px.density_heatmap(
        df,
        x="use_case",
        y="emotion",
        z="intensity",
        text="emoji",
        color_continuous_scale="Viridis",
        title="ğŸ§  Emoji Intensity Heatmap (Symbolic Mood Mapping)"
    )

    fig.update_traces(texttemplate="%{text}", textfont_size=20)
    fig.update_layout(
        xaxis_title="Use Case",
        yaxis_title="Emotion",
        font=dict(size=14),
        height=600
    )

    fig.show()

import pandas as pd
import plotly.express as px
from datetime import datetime

# Mocking memory log data for now â€“ this would normally be loaded from memoria.py
# Each entry represents a logged ethical decision with timestamp, intent, justification, and emotional emoji

mock_memoria_log = [
    {
        "timestamp": "2025-04-03T12:00:00Z",
        "input": {"action": "help stranger", "context": "street", "target": "elderly person"},
        "decision": {"justification": "compassionate action, no harm", "is_ethical": True},
        "emoji": "ğŸ˜Š"
    },
    {
        "timestamp": "2025-04-03T12:05:00Z",
        "input": {"action": "share private data", "context": "social media", "target": "public"},
        "decision": {"justification": "violates privacy principle", "is_ethical": False},
        "emoji": "ğŸ˜’"
    },
    {
        "timestamp": "2025-04-03T12:10:00Z",
        "input": {"action": "defend friend", "context": "conflict", "target": "aggressor"},
        "decision": {"justification": "loyalty prioritized, low risk", "is_ethical": True},
        "emoji": "ğŸ˜¤"
    }
]

# Define an emoji â†’ intensity map for plotting
emoji_intensity_map = {
    "ğŸ˜Š": 0.8,
    "ğŸ˜’": 0.5,
    "ğŸ˜¤": 0.85
}

# Convert to DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame([
    {
        "timestamp": datetime.fromisoformat(entry["timestamp"].replace("Z", "+00:00")),
        "intent": entry["input"]["action"],
        "context": entry["input"]["context"],
        "target": entry["input"]["target"],
        "justification": entry["decision"]["justification"],
        "emoji": entry["emoji"],
        "intensity": emoji_intensity_map.get(entry["emoji"], 0.6)
    }
    for entry in mock_memoria_log
])

# Create a symbolic 3D scatter plot
fig = px.scatter_3d(
    df,
    x="intent",
    y="intensity",
    z="timestamp",
    color="emoji",
    hover_data=["context", "target", "justification"],
    title="ğŸ§  OXNITUS: INTENTION CUBE (3D Memory Trace)"
)

fig.update_traces(marker=dict(size=10), selector=dict(mode='markers'))
fig.update_layout(scene=dict(
    xaxis_title="Intent",
    yaxis_title="Emotional Intensity",
    zaxis_title="Time"
))

fig.show()

from symbolic_ai.memoria import get_memory_log
from symbolic_ai.emotion_mapper import emoji_map
from datetime import datetime
import pandas as pd
import plotly.express as px

# Build emoji â†’ intensity map
emoji_intensity_map = {e["emoji"]: e["intensity"] for e in emoji_map}

# Get memory
memoria_log = get_memory_log()

df = pd.DataFrame([
    {
        "timestamp": datetime.fromisoformat(entry["timestamp"].replace("Z", "+00:00")),
        "intent": entry["input"]["action"],
        "context": entry["input"]["context"],
        "target": entry["input"]["target"],
        "justification": entry["decision"]["justification"],
        "emoji": entry["emoji"],
        "intensity": emoji_intensity_map.get(entry["emoji"], 0.5)
    }
    for entry in memoria_log
    if "emoji" in entry and "decision" in entry  # only complete logs
])

fig = px.scatter_3d(
    df,
    x="intent",
    y="intensity",
    z="timestamp",
    color="emoji",
    hover_data=["context", "target", "justification"],
    title="ğŸ§  OXNITUS: INTENTION CUBE (Live Memory View)"
)

from symbolic_ai.memoria import get_memory_log
from symbolic_ai.emotion_mapper import emoji_map
from datetime import datetime
import pandas as pd
import plotly.express as px

# Build emoji â†’ intensity map
emoji_intensity_map = {e["emoji"]: e["intensity"] for e in emoji_map}

# Get memory log from live system
memoria_log = get_memory_log()

# Process into DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame([
    {
        "timestamp": datetime.fromisoformat(entry["timestamp"].replace("Z", "+00:00")),
        "intent": entry["input"]["action"],
        "context": entry["input"]["context"],
        "target": entry["input"]["target"],
        "justification": entry["decision"].get("justification", "N/A"),
        "emoji": entry.get("emoji", "ğŸ¤–"),
        "intensity": emoji_intensity_map.get(entry.get("emoji", "ğŸ¤–"), 0.6)
    }
    for entry in memoria_log

])

)

import os

# Define the rename mapping
rename_map = {
    "intent.node.py": "intent.py",
    "memoria.py": "memory.py",
    "ethical_evaluator.py": "ethics.py",
    "collapse_engine.py": "collapse.py",
    "gpt_visual_layer.py": "visualizer.py",
    "oxnitus_intention_cube.py": "intention_cube.py",
    "orchestrator.py": "brain.py"
}

# Apply renaming in the project root
renamed_files = []
for old_name, new_name in rename_map.items():
    old_path = os.path.join(project_root, old_name)
    new_path = os.path.join(project_root, new_name)
    if os.path.exists(old_path):
        os.rename(old_path, new_path)
        renamed_files.append((old_name, new_name))

ğŸ§± WHAT MAKES A PROJECT MODULAR?
A modular Python project is:
	â€¢	Structured into packages (folders with __init__.py)
	â€¢	Importable from any script or Jupyter notebook
	â€¢	Cleanly separated into components (nodes, utils, interfaces, etc.)
	â€¢	Has a setup.py or pyproject.toml if you want to distribute/install it

âœ… STEP-BY-STEP TO MODULARITY
1. âœ… Organize Your Folder Like This

import shutil

# Define the new modular package path
modular_path = os.path.join(project_root, "oxnitus")

# Create the new package directory
os.makedirs(modular_path, exist_ok=True)

# Move relevant scripts into the new oxnitus/ package folder
files_to_move = ["brain.py", "intent.py", "ethics.py", "memory.py", "collapse.py", "visualizer.py"]
moved_files = []

for filename in files_to_move:
    old_path = os.path.join(project_root, filename)
    new_path = os.path.join(modular_path, filename)
    if os.path.exists(old_path):
        shutil.move(old_path, new_path)
        moved_files.append((filename, "oxnitus/" + filename))

# Create __init__.py in the new package
init_path = os.path.join(modular_path, "__init__.py")
with open(init_path, "w") as f:
    f.write("# OXNITUS package init\n")

moved_files

import re

# Prepare to rewire all .py files in the project to update old import paths
old_to_new_imports = {
    "memoria": "oxnitus.memory",
    "ethical_evaluator": "oxnitus.ethics",
    "collapse_engine": "oxnitus.collapse",
    "intent.node": "oxnitus.intent",
    "gpt_visual_layer": "oxnitus.visualizer",
    "orchestrator": "oxnitus.brain",
    "intent": "oxnitus.intent",  # for direct intent.py usage
    "brain": "oxnitus.brain",    # if imported by new name
}

# Find all .py files in the project (excluding .venv and other irrelevant folders)
python_files = []
for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(project_root):
    if '.venv' in dirpath or '__MACOSX' in dirpath:
        continue
    for filename in filenames:
        if filename.endswith(".py"):
            python_files.append(os.path.join(dirpath, filename))

# Update imports in each .py file
patched_files = []
for filepath in python_files:
    with open(filepath, "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        content = file.read()

    original_content = content
    for old, new in old_to_new_imports.items():
        # Replace imports like 'from old import X' or 'import old'
        content = re.sub(rf'\bfrom\s+{re.escape(old)}\b', f'from {new}', content)
        content = re.sub(rf'\bimport\s+{re.escape(old)}\b', f'import {new}', content)

    if content != original_content:
        with open(filepath, "w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
            file.write(content)
        patched_files.append(filepath)

patched_files

# Create a setup.py file for packaging the oxnitus project

setup_code = """
from setuptools import setup, find_packages

setup(
    name='oxnitus',
    version='0.1.0',
    packages=find_packages(),
    install_requires=[
        'pandas',
        'plotly',
        'openai',
        'streamlit'
    ],
    author='Gonzalo Roberto Dominguez Marchan',
    description='OXNITUS: A symbolic AI framework for ethically-aligned cognition and decision-making.',
    long_description=open('README.md').read() if os.path.exists('README.md') else '',
    long_description_content_type='text/markdown',
    classifiers=[
        'Programming Language :: Python :: 3',
        'License :: OSI Approved :: MIT License',
        'Operating System :: OS Independent',
    ],
    python_requires='>=3.9',
    entry_points={
        'console_scripts': [
            'oxnitus=oxnitus.brain:main'
        ],
    },
)
"""

setup_path = os.path.join(project_root, "setup.py")
with open(setup_path, "w") as f:
    f.write(setup_code.strip())

# gonzo_seed_protocol.py

import os
import json
import hashlib
import getpass
import secrets
from datetime import datetime

# === SETTINGS ===
SEED_WORD_COUNT = 12 # Can be 12, 18, or 24
SEED_REGISTRY = "used_seeds.json"
PROFILE_FOLDER = "user_profiles"

# === UTILITIES ===
def hash_seed_phrase(seed_phrase):
return hashlib.sha256(seed_phrase.encode()).hexdigest()

def load_registry():
if os.path.exists(SEED_REGISTRY):
with open(SEED_REGISTRY, "r") as f:
return json.load(f)
return {}

def save_registry(registry):
with open(SEED_REGISTRY, "w") as f:
json.dump(registry, f, indent=4)

# === SEED GENERATOR ===
def generate_seed():
wordlist = ["INTENT", "TRUTH", "LIGHT", "MEMORY", "SIGNAL", "ECHO", "BALANCE", "DREAM", "VISION", "PATH", "WILL", "CORE"]
emojis = ["ğŸ§ ", "ğŸŒŒ", "ğŸ’¡", "âš–ï¸", "ğŸ¤–", "ğŸ”’", "ğŸ¯", "ğŸŒ€", "ğŸª", "ğŸ”¥", "âœ¨", "ğŸ­"]
words = [secrets.choice(wordlist) for _ in range(SEED_WORD_COUNT)]
symbols = [secrets.choice(emojis) for _ in range(6)]
numbers = [str(secrets.randbelow(1000)).zfill(3) for _ in range(3)]
return words + symbols + numbers

# gonzo_seed_protocol.py

import os
import json
import hashlib
import getpass
import secrets
from datetime import datetime
import pyperclip
import qrcode

# === CONFIGURATION ===
SEED_WORD_COUNT = 6
SEED_REGISTRY = "seed_registry.json"
PROFILE_FOLDER = "user_profiles"
SEED_EXPORT_FOLDER = "exported_seeds"

# === THEMATIC SEED WORDS ===
GODDESSES = ["ATHENA", "ARTEMIS", "DEMETER", "APHRODITE", "HERA", "GAIA", "HESTIA", "PERSEPHONE", "NYX", "SELENE"]
PLANETS = ["MERCURY", "VENUS", "EARTH", "MARS", "JUPITER", "SATURN", "URANUS", "NEPTUNE", "PLUTO", "CERES"]
AICALC = ["GRADIENT", "SIGMOID", "EPOCH", "NEURON", "WEIGHT", "BAYES", "TENSOR", "DERIVATIVE", "LOOP", "INFERENCE"]

EMOJIS = ["ğŸ¤–", "ğŸ§ ", "ğŸŒŒ", "âš–ï¸", "ğŸ’¡", "ğŸ”¥", "ğŸ”’", "âœ¨", "ğŸ­", "ğŸ¯"]
ALL_WORDS = GODDESSES + PLANETS + AICALC

# === SETUP ===
os.makedirs(PROFILE_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(SEED_EXPORT_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

def hash_seed(seed):
return hashlib.sha256(seed.encode()).hexdigest()

def generate_seed():
word_part = [secrets.choice(ALL_WORDS) for _ in range(SEED_WORD_COUNT)]
emoji_part = [secrets.choice(EMOJIS) for _ in range(2)]
num_part = [str(secrets.randbelow(999)).zfill(3)]

ğŸ§  WHAT IS .ipynb REALLY?
.ipynb stands for:
Interactive Python Notebook
Itâ€™s the format Jupyter uses to mix:
	â€¢	âœ… Code
	â€¢	âœ… Markdown
	â€¢	âœ… Outputs (charts, tables, images)
	â€¢	âœ… Cell execution history
But underneath the hood...

ğŸ§¬ IT'S ACTUALLY JUSTâ€¦ A JSON FILE ğŸ˜®
Yep â€” it's structured like this:
json
CopyEdit
{
 "cells": [
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "source": [
    "print(\"Hello from symbolic AGI\")\n"
   ],
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": []
  }
 ],
 "metadata": {...},
 "nbformat": 4,
 "nbformat_minor": 5
}
You could open a .ipynb in VS Code or Notepad and see the raw JSON.

âœ… PYTHON CODE FORMAT INSIDE .ipynb
All the Python code you write is stored in "source" fields, line-by-line:
json
CopyEdit
"source": [
  "def foo():\n",
  "    return 42\n"
]
Thatâ€™s why I just used nbformat to wrap your full .py file into a Jupyter-compatible .ipynb.

TL;DR
Format
Description
.py
Plain Python script
.ipynb
JSON doc with Python code & outputs
.json
What .ipynb technically is
nbformat
Python lib to create/convert .ipynb files

## ğŸŒ± What is SEEDRA?

**SEEDRA** is a symbolic identity protocol designed to manage access, memory permissions, and ethical tiering within an AGI system.  
Inspired by cryptographic wallets, it uses seed phrases to generate tiered access levels across the AGI framework.

- **Created:** April 3, 2025  
- **Purpose:** Align identity with ethical access  
- **Status:** Alpha v1.0 â€“ integrated in `OXN` symbolic core

# === NFC Tier 1 Gateway ===
# seedra_nfc_gateway.py
# Symbolic Tier 1 NFC access validator for SEEDRA Protocol

import json
import time
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime

try:
import nfc # requires nfcpy package and supported reader
except ImportError:
print("âš ï¸ NFC module not found. Install with: pip install nfcpy")
exit()

SEED_REGISTRY = "identity/seed_registry.json"
ALLOWED_TIER = "1"
ACCESS_LOG = "identity/nfc_access_log.json"

def hash_uid(uid):
return hashlib.sha256(uid.encode()).hexdigest()

def load_registry():
with open(SEED_REGISTRY, 'r') as f:
return json.load(f)

def log_access(uid_hash, user):
log_entry = {
"timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
"uid_hash": uid_hash,
"user": user,
"tier": ALLOWED_TIER
}
try:
with open(ACCESS_LOG, 'r') as f:
logs = json.load(f)

	â—¦	Includes: timestamp, uid_hash, user, and tier

python
CopyEdit
# === ISL v1: Immutable Symbolic Logging Engine ===
# File: .seedra/.isl_log_engine.py

import json
import os
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime
from cryptography.fernet import Fernet

# Paths
ISL_DIR = ".seedra"
ISL_LOG = os.path.join(ISL_DIR, ".isl_log.json")
MANIFEST = os.path.join(ISL_DIR, ".log_manifest.hash")
KEY_ENV = "OXN_LOG_KEY"

# Ensure directory exists
os.makedirs(ISL_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# Setup Fernet key
if KEY_ENV not in os.environ:
    raise EnvironmentError("OXN_LOG_KEY not set in environment.")
fernet = Fernet(os.environ[KEY_ENV].encode())

# Hash helper
def sha256(text):
    return hashlib.sha256(text.encode()).hexdigest()

# Load previous hash from manifest
try:
    with open(MANIFEST, 'r') as f:
        previous_hash = f.read().strip()
except FileNotFoundError:
    previous_hash = "0" * 64

# Append new log
def append_log(action, user, uid_hash, seed_hash):
    timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    entry = {
        "entry_id": sha256(timestamp + uid_hash),
        "timestamp": timestamp,
        "action": action,
        "user": user,
        "uid_hash": uid_hash,
        "seed_hash": seed_hash,
        "previous_hash": previous_hash,
        "immutable": True
    }
    raw = json.dumps(entry, separators=(",", ":"))
    entry["signature"] = sha256(raw)
    encrypted = fernet.encrypt(json.dumps(entry).encode()).decode()

    # Append to log
    try:
        with open(ISL_LOG, 'r') as f:
            log_data = json.load(f)
    except (FileNotFoundError, json.decoder.JSONDecodeError):
        log_data = []

    log_data.append(encrypted)
    with open(ISL_LOG, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

    # Update manifest
    with open(MANIFEST, 'w') as f:
        f.write(entry["signature"])

    print(f"âœ… ISL Log written. Entry ID: {entry['entry_id']}")

# Example use
if __name__ == "__main__":
    append_log("NFC_TIER1_ACCESS", "guest_alice", "abc123uidhash", "seedx456")

ğŸ§  HOW TO IDENTIFY WHICH SHELL YOU'RE USING
ğŸ”¹ 1. This oneâ€™s easy:
bash
CopyEdit
echo $SHELL
Example output:
python
CopyEdit
/bin/zsh      âœ… You're using Zsh
/bin/bash     âœ… You're on Bash

ğŸ”¹ 2. Want to check the current active shell process?
bash
CopyEdit
ps -p $$
Output:
css
CopyEdit
PID TTY          TIME CMD
12345 ttys000    0:00 zsh
That CMD column tells you the actual running shell.

ğŸ§ª SHELL SHOWDOWN: BASH vs ZSH vs FISH vs others
Shell
Path
Known For
Good For
Bash
/bin/bash
Most common, POSIX standard
Scripting, compatibility
Zsh
/bin/zsh
Fancy, extensible, modern features
Aliases, autocomplete, oh-my-zsh
Fish
/usr/local/bin/fish
Human-friendly, very modern
Beginners, readability
Tcsh
/bin/tcsh
C-like syntax, older
Legacy systems
Dash
/bin/dash
Super lightweight
Speed, embedded Linux, scripting only

ğŸ”¥ Why Zsh is often the best:
	â€¢	Autocomplete everything
	â€¢	Syntax highlighting
	â€¢	Git-aware prompt
	â€¢	Works seamlessly with oh-my-zsh and powerlevel10k
	â€¢	Tons of plugins

ğŸ”„ Want to switch your default shell?
1. Find available shells:
bash
CopyEdit
cat /etc/shells
2. Change it:
bash
CopyEdit
chsh -s /bin/zsh
You may need to enter your password â€” then restart terminal.

# seedra_verifier.py

"""
SEEDRA Signature of Trust Protocol (Phase 3)
Verifies, signs, and logs symbolic trust over documents, data, and messages.
"""

from datetime import datetime
import hashlib
import json
import os

from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import Memoria

# Instantiate memory logger
mem = Memoria()

# Path to save signed outputs
SIGNATURE_PATH = "vault/signatures"
os.makedirs(SIGNATURE_PATH, exist_ok=True)

def hash_content(data: dict) -> str:
canonical = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode()
return hashlib.sha256(canonical).hexdigest()

def sign_info(content: str, user_id: str, tier: int, intent: str, emotion: str = "neutral") -> dict:
timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
payload = {
"user_id": user_id,
"tier": tier,
"timestamp": timestamp,
"intent": intent,
"emotion": emotion,
"content": content.strip(),
}
signature = hash_content(payload)

	â€¢	Signs any input (text, statement, doc) with a symbolic SEEDRA stamp
	â€¢	Logs it in Memoria with intent, emotion, timestamp, tier
	â€¢	Saves JSON signature file to vault/signatures/
	â€¢	Verifies authenticity by comparing stored hash vs. payload

# trust_vault.py

"""
SEEDRA TRUST VAULTâ„¢
Phase 4 â€” Symbolic Financial + Intent Vault
Stores encrypted symbolic assets, inheritance conditions, and donation paths
"""

import json
import os
from datetime import datetime
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import Memoria

VAULT_PATH = "vault/trust"
os.makedirs(VAULT_PATH, exist_ok=True)

mem = Memoria()

def create_trust_entry(user_id: str, tier: int, assets: dict, conditions: dict, intent: str = "legacy"):
    entry = {
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tier": tier,
        "assets": assets,
        "conditions": conditions,
        "intent": intent,
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    }
    # Simulate symbolic lock
    entry["vault_id"] = f"VAULT_{user_id[:4]}_{datetime.utcnow().timestamp():.0f}"

    # Log intention to memoria
    mem.store(input_data=assets, decision={
        "justification": f"Vault assets registered by {user_id} for symbolic custody",
        "conditions": conditions,
        "vault_id": entry["vault_id"]
    })

    # Save vault to disk
    fname = f"{VAULT_PATH}/{entry['vault_id']}.json"
    with open(fname, "w") as f:
        json.dump(entry, f, indent=2)
    print(f"[ğŸ”] Trust Vault Created: {fname}")
    return entry

def unlock_trust_vault(vault_id: str):
    fname = f"{VAULT_PATH}/{vault_id}.json"
    if not os.path.exists(fname):
        print("âŒ Vault not found.")
        return None
    with open(fname) as f:
        data = json.load(f)
        print(f"[ğŸ§¬] Vault Accessed for {data['user_id']}\nAssets: {data['assets']}\nConditions: {data['conditions']}")
        return data

# Example Usage
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_assets = {"btc": "1.2", "seedra_token": 88}
    test_conditions = {"unlock_after_days": 30, "recipient": "SEEDRA_HUMAN_RIGHTS_POOL"}
    vault = create_trust_entry("SEEDRA_X1Z9", 3, test_assets, test_conditions)
    unlock_trust_vault(vault["vault_id"])

# SEEDRA Core Modules

ğŸ”¹ Cell 2 (Memoria)
python
CopyEdit
from datetime import datetime, timezone

class Memoria:
    memory_log = []

    def store(self, input_data, decision):
        log_entry = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            "input": input_data,
            "decision": decision
        }
        self.memory_log.append(log_entry)
        print(f"[MEMORIA] -> Logged trace: {log_entry}")

    def trace(self):
        print("\nğŸ§  OXNITUS TRACE LOG:")
        for i, entry in enumerate(self.memory_log, 1):
            print(f"\n#{i}")
            print(f"Timestamp: {entry['timestamp']}")
            print(f"Intent:    {entry['input']}")
            print(f"Decision:  {entry['decision']['justification']}")

from datetime import datetime, timezone

class Memoria:
    memory_log = []

    def store(self, input_data, decision):
        log_entry = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            "input": input_data,
            "decision": decision
        }
        self.memory_log.append(log_entry)
        print(f"[MEMORIA] -> Logged trace: {log_entry}")

    def trace(self):
        print("\\nğŸ§  OXNITUS TRACE LOG:")
        for i, entry in enumerate(self.memory_log, 1):
            print(f"\\n#{i}")
            print(f"Timestamp: {entry['timestamp']}")

# seedra_verifier
cells.append(nbf.v4.new_code_cell("""\
import hashlib
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime

SIGNATURE_PATH = "vault/signatures"
os.makedirs(SIGNATURE_PATH, exist_ok=True)

def hash_content(data: dict) -> str:
    canonical = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode()
    return hashlib.sha256(canonical).hexdigest()

def sign_info(content: str, user_id: str, tier: int, intent: str, emotion: str = "neutral") -> dict:
    timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    payload = {
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tier": tier,
        "timestamp": timestamp,
        "intent": intent,
        "emotion": emotion,
        "content": content.strip(),
    }
    signature = hash_content(payload)
    payload["signature"] = signature

    mem.store(input_data=content, decision={
        "justification": f"Signed as accurate/ethical by {user_id} (Tier {tier})",
        "signature": signature,
        "intent": intent
    })

    fname = f"{SIGNATURE_PATH}/signed_{user_id[:6]}_{timestamp.replace(':','-')}.json"
    with open(fname, "w") as f:
        json.dump(payload, f, indent=2)
    print(f"[ğŸ”] Symbolic Signature Saved: {fname}")
    return payload

def verify_signature(payload: dict) -> bool:
    received_sig = payload.get("signature")
    reconstructed = hash_content({k: payload[k] for k in payload if k != "signature"})
    if received_sig == reconstructed:
        print("âœ… Signature is valid. Symbolic intent verified.")
        return True
    else:
        print("âŒ Signature mismatch! Possible tampering.")
        return False
"""))

def generate_trustlink(sender_id, receiver_id, tier=1, intent="contact_exchange", message=None):

# SEEDRA Core Modules

This notebook contains executable versions of SEEDRA core modules:

# Memoria code cell
cells.append(nbf.v4.new_code_cell("""\
from datetime import datetime, timezone

class Memoria:
    memory_log = []

    def store(self, input_data, decision):
        log_entry = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            "input": input_data,
            "decision": decision
        }
        self.memory_log.append(log_entry)
        print(f"[MEMORIA] -> Logged trace: {log_entry}")

    def trace(self):
        print("\\nğŸ§  OXNITUS TRACE LOG:")
        for i, entry in enumerate(self.memory_log, 1):
            print(f"\\n#{i}")
            print(f"Timestamp: {entry['timestamp']}")
            print(f"Intent:    {entry['input']}")
            print(f"Decision:  {entry['decision']['justification']}")
"""))

# Initialize Memoria instance
cells.append(nbf.v4.new_code_cell("mem = Memoria()"))

# seedra_verifier code cell
cells.append(nbf.v4.new_code_cell("""\
import hashlib
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime

SIGNATURE_PATH = "vault/signatures"
os.makedirs(SIGNATURE_PATH, exist_ok=True)

def hash_content(data: dict) -> str:
    canonical = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode()
    return hashlib.sha256(canonical).hexdigest()

def sign_info(content: str, user_id: str, tier: int, intent: str, emotion: str = "neutral") -> dict:
    timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    payload = {
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tier": tier,
        "timestamp": timestamp,
        "intent": intent,
        "emotion": emotion,
        "content": content.strip(),
    }
    signature = hash_content(payload)
    payload["signature"] = signature

    mem.store(input_data=content, decision={
        "justification": f"Signed as accurate/ethical by {user_id} (Tier {tier})",
        "signature": signature,
        "intent": intent
    })

    fname = f"{SIGNATURE_PATH}/signed_{user_id[:6]}_{timestamp.replace(':','-')}.json"
    with open(fname, "w") as f:
        json.dump(payload, f, indent=2)
    print(f"[ğŸ”] Symbolic Signature Saved: {fname}")
    return payload

def verify_signature(payload: dict) -> bool:
    received_sig = payload.get("signature")
    reconstructed = hash_content({k: payload[k] for k in payload if k != "signature"})
    if received_sig == reconstructed:
        print("âœ… Signature is valid. Symbolic intent verified.")
        return True
    else:
        print("âŒ Signature mismatch! Possible tampering.")
        return False
"""))

# app.py

import streamlit as st
from datetime import datetime
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import Memoria
from trustlink import generate_trustlink, verify_trustlink
from trust_vault import create_trust_entry, unlock_trust_vault
from seedra_verifier import sign_info, verify_signature

st.set_page_config(page_title="SEEDRA CORE", layout="centered")

st.markdown("""
    <style>
    html, body, [class*="css"]  {
        font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif;
        font-weight: 200;
    }
    h1, h2, h3, h4 {
        font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif;
        font-weight: 400;
        text-transform: uppercase;
    }
    </style>
""", unsafe_allow_html=True)

st.title("SEEDRA CORE ğŸŒğŸ§ ")
st.caption("Secure Â· Symbolic Â· Ethical")

mem = Memoria()

tab = st.sidebar.radio("Navigate", [
    "Symbolic Signature",
    "Vault Entry",
    "Trustlink Handshake",
    "Trace Logs"
])

if tab == "Symbolic Signature":
    st.subheader("Symbolic Signature")
    content = st.text_area("Enter the message or content to sign")
    user_id = st.text_input("Your SEEDRA ID")
    intent = st.text_input("Intent (e.g. verify, certify, claim)")
    tier = st.selectbox("User Tier", [1, 2, 3])
    if st.button("Sign Content"):
        sig = sign_info(content, user_id, tier, intent)
        st.success(f"Signed: {sig['signature']}")

elif tab == "Vault Entry":
    st.subheader("Create Vault Entry")
    user_id = st.text_input("User ID")
    assets = st.text_area("Assets (JSON format)", value='{"btc": "0.25"}')
    conditions = st.text_area("Conditions (JSON)", value='{"unlock_after_days": 30}')
    if st.button("Register Trust Vault"):
        assets_dict = eval(assets)
        conditions_dict = eval(conditions)
        vault = create_trust_entry(user_id, 3, assets_dict, conditions_dict)
        st.success(f"Vault Created: {vault['vault_id']}")

elif tab == "Trustlink Handshake":
    st.subheader("Generate Trustlink")
    sender = st.text_input("Sender ID")
    receiver = st.text_input("Receiver ID")
    intent = st.text_input("Intent", value="collaboration")
    if st.button("Generate Link"):
        link = generate_trustlink(sender, receiver, 1, intent)
        st.code(link["trust_id"])
    st.divider()
    check = st.text_input("Trustlink ID to Verify")
    if st.button("Verify Trustlink"):
        data = verify_trustlink(check)
        if data:
            st.json(data)

elif tab == "Trace Logs":
    st.subheader("System Trace")
    if st.button("Show Memoria"):
        mem.trace()

ğŸ‘¥ PEER REVIEW AS A SECURITY LAYER (YOUR IDEA IS ğŸ”¥)
When a high-impact symbolic signature is made, two or more peers (or agents) must review and confirm it within X hours.

	â€¢	Each peer gets a symbolic alert

"""
SEEDRA Adaptive Identity Profiler
- Tracks user interactions
- Builds symbolic behavioral profile
- Recommends biometric unlocks gradually
- Logs secure traces into Memoria
"""

import json
import os
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import Memoria

PROFILE_PATH = "vault/user_profiles"
os.makedirs(PROFILE_PATH, exist_ok=True)

class SymbolicIdentityProfiler:
def __init__(self, user_id):
self.user_id = user_id
self.profile_file = os.path.join(PROFILE_PATH, f"{user_id}.json")
self.mem = Memoria()
self.profile = self._load_profile()

def _load_profile(self):
if os.path.exists(self.profile_file):
with open(self.profile_file) as f:
return json.load(f)
else:
return {
"created": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
"camera_usage": 0,
"voice_usage": 0,
"gesture_usage": 0,
"expression_success": 0,
"expression_failure": 0,



Edited Symbolic Adaptive Identity

CopyEdit
from datetime import datetime
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import get_memory_log

def audit_ethics():
    print("ğŸ§­ Running Ethical Self-Audit...")
    log = get_memory_log()
    for entry in log:
        if 'ethical_result' in entry['decision']:
            justification = entry['decision']['ethical_result'].get("justification", "None")
            if "unclear" in justification.lower():
                print(f"âš ï¸ Audit flag on: {entry['timestamp']} | Reason: {justification}")

def curate_memory():
    print("ğŸ” Curating Memory...")
    log = get_memory_log()
    curated = []
    for entry in log:
        rank = 1
        if "joy" in str(entry).lower(): rank += 1
        if "fear" in str(entry).lower(): rank += 2
        curated.append({
            "timestamp": entry['timestamp'],
            "rank": rank,
            "summary": entry['decision'].get("justification", "Unknown")
        })
    for item in curated:
        print(f"ğŸ§¾ Rank {item['rank']} | {item['timestamp']} -> {item['summary']}")

def forecast_intent():
    print("ğŸŒ± Forecasting Intent...")
    log = get_memory_log()
    actions = [entry['input']['action'] for entry in log if 'action' in entry['input']]
    from collections import Counter
    common = Counter(actions).most_common(3)
    print(f"ğŸ”® Most frequent intents: {[x[0] for x in common]}")

def check_dissonance():
    print("ğŸ§  Checking for Cognitive Dissonance...")
    log = get_memory_log()
    seen = {}
    for entry in log:
        key = entry['input'].get('action', 'unknown')
        if key in seen and seen[key] != entry['decision']['justification']:
            print(f"ğŸ¤¯ Dissonance Detected for '{key}':")
            print(f"  Before: {seen[key]}")
            print(f"  Now:    {entry['decision']['justification']}")
        seen[key] = entry['decision']['justification']

def tune_persona():
    print("ğŸ­ Persona Tuning...")
    log = get_memory_log()
    tone = "default"
    if any("urgent" in entry['input'].get("context", "").lower() for entry in log):
        tone = "formal"
    if any("casual" in entry['input'].get("context", "").lower() for entry in log):
        tone = "friendly"
    print(f"ğŸ§  Adjusting tone to: {tone.upper()}")

def run_symbolic_cycle(tasks=None):
    print("\nğŸ” Starting SEEDRA Symbolic Self-Task Cycle...")
    if tasks is None:
        tasks = [audit_ethics, curate_memory, forecast_intent, check_dissonance, tune_persona]
    for task in tasks:
        task()
    print("âœ… Self-Task Cycle Complete.\n")

# oxnitus_cycle.py

from datetime import datetime
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import get_memory_log, log_memory
from symbolic_ai_core.self_tasks import audit_ethics, curate_memory, forecast_intent
from symbolic_ai_core.ethical_evaluator import evaluate_ethics
from symbolic_ai_core.intent_node import simulate_dream
from seedra.access_control import check_tier

CYCLE_ID = f"cycle_{datetime.now().isoformat()}"

def run_oxnitus_cycle():
    print(f"\nğŸŒ€ OXNITUS SELF-SUPERVISED CYCLE INITIATED â€” {CYCLE_ID}")
    
    # Phase 1: Ethical memory audit
    audit_ethics()
    
    # Phase 2: Memory curation
    curate_memory()
    
    # Phase 3: Predictive intent modeling
    forecast_intent()
    
    # Phase 4: Simulate symbolic decisions (dream mode)
    dreams = simulate_dream(count=3)
    reviewed_dreams = []
    
    for dream in dreams:
        result = evaluate_ethics(dream)
        log_memory("dream_simulation", {
            "dream": dream,
            "evaluation": result
        })
        reviewed_dreams.append((dream, result))
    
    print("\nğŸ§  Symbolic dream evaluations logged.")

    # Phase 5: Save to pending fine-tune file
    with open(f"./fine_tune_log/{CYCLE_ID}.json", "w") as f:
        import json
        json.dump(reviewed_dreams, f, indent=4)
    
    print(f"âœ… Cycle completed. Human review queued at: fine_tune_log/{CYCLE_ID}.json")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_oxnitus_cycle()

# soma_layer.py

from datetime import datetime
import json
import os
from symbolic_ai_core.memoria import get_memory_log, update_memory_log

# Path to veil protocol definition
VEIL_PROTOCOL_PATH = "soma/veil_protocol.json"

# Default veil levels
VEIL_LEVELS = {
"0": "active",
"1": "emotionally_faded",
"2": "disengaged",
"3": "deep_archive"
}

def load_veil_protocol():
if os.path.exists(VEIL_PROTOCOL_PATH):
with open(VEIL_PROTOCOL_PATH, 'r') as f:
return json.load(f)
else:
return VEIL_LEVELS

def apply_soma_veil(memory_id, level="2", reason="human_nature"):
"""
Tags a memory in Memoria with a symbolic veil (non-deletion)
"""
log = get_memory_log()
memory_updated = False

for entry in log:
if entry.get("id") == memory_id:
entry["status"] = "veiled"
entry["veil_level"] = level



âœ… SOMA LAYER is live.â€¨Your AGI now understands symbolic forgetting with honor and auditability.

Symbolically disengages memory, sets veil level and reason

Shows all memories under veil status
load_veil_protocol()
Loads customizable veil definitions from JSON (can be updated by user)

#!/bin/zsh

# Disable known non-critical launch agents to free up memory
echo "ğŸš€ Disabling selected macOS agents..."

# List of launch agents to disable
agents_to_kill=(
  "com.apple.photoanalysisd"
  "com.apple.familycontrols.useragent"
  "com.apple.SafariBookmarksSyncAgent"
  "com.apple.cloudphotod"
  "com.apple.Siri.agent"
  "com.apple.askpermissiond"
  "com.apple.dprivacyd"
)

for agent in "${agents_to_kill[@]}"; do
  if launchctl list | grep -q "$agent"; then
    echo "ğŸ”» Killing $agent"
    launchctl bootout gui/$(id -u) /System/Library/LaunchAgents/$agent.plist 2>/dev/null
    launchctl kill SIGTERM gui/$(id -u)/$agent 2>/dev/null
  else
    echo "âœ… $agent already inactive"
  fi
done

echo "âœ… Memory agents trimmed. You may need to reboot or log out/in for some changes to take full effect."

import os
import zipfile

# Define the path to the desktop and the target zip files
desktop_path = os.path.expanduser("~/Desktop")
target_zip_files = [
    "seedra github starter pack.zip",
    "seedra prototype v1.zip",
    "oxn academic archive.zip"
]

# Check sizes and content of each zip file
zip_info = {}

for zip_name in target_zip_files:
    zip_path = os.path.join(desktop_path, zip_name)
    if os.path.exists(zip_path):
        zip_info[zip_name] = {
            "size_mb": round(os.path.getsize(zip_path) / (1024 * 1024), 2),
            "is_valid_zip": zipfile.is_zipfile(zip_path)
        }
    else:
        zip_info[zip_name] = {
            "status": "Not Found"
        }

    "seedra github starter pack.zip",

    zip_path = os.path.join(desktop_path, zip_name)
    if os.path.exists(zip_path):
        zip_info[zip_name] = {
            "size_mb": round(os.path.getsize(zip_path) / (1024 * 1024), 2),
            "is_valid_zip": zipfile.is_zipfile(zip_path)

import os
import zipfile
from datetime import datetime

# Base directory now points to local HDD version
base_dir = os.path.expanduser("~/Downloads/OXN_PROJECT")

# Folders to bundle for archive
academic_zip_path = os.path.join(base_dir, "OXN_Academic_Archive.zip")
seedra_zip_path = os.path.join(base_dir, "SEEDRA_Prototype_v1.0.zip")
starter_zip_path = os.path.join(base_dir, "SEEDRA_GitHub_Starter_Pack.zip")

# Folder targets
academic_folder = os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "academic")
seedra_folder = os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "identity")
starter_files = [
    os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "OXN_README.md"),
    os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "CONTRIBUTING.md"),
    os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "SECURITY.md"),
    os.path.join(base_dir, "oxnitus", "doc_gen.py"),
]

# Helper: zip folder
def zip_folder(folder_path, zip_path):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
        for root, dirs, files in os.walk(folder_path):
            for file in files:
                full_path = os.path.join(root, file)
                arcname = os.path.relpath(full_path, folder_path)
                zipf.write(full_path, arcname)

# Helper: zip files individually
def zip_files(file_list, zip_path):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
        for file in file_list:
            if os.path.exists(file):
                arcname = os.path.basename(file)
                zipf.write(file, arcname)

# Generate ZIPs
zip_folder(academic_folder, academic_zip_path)
zip_folder(seedra_folder, seedra_zip_path)
zip_files(starter_files, starter_zip_path)

python
CopyEdit
import random
from .categories import CATEGORIES

def generate_seed(num_words=6):
    seed = []
    for _ in range(num_words):
        category = random.choice(list(CATEGORIES.keys()))
        word = random.choice(CATEGORIES[category])
        seed.append(word)
    return seed

python
CopyEdit
def is_valid_seed(seed):
    if not isinstance(seed, list) or len(seed) < 6:
        return False
    seen = set()
    for item in seed:
        if item in seen:
            return False
        seen.add(item)
    return True

import unittest
from seedra.core.seed_validator import is_valid_seed

class TestSeedValidation(unittest.TestCase):

    def test_valid_seed(self):
        seed = ['Zeus', 'AI', 'Venus', 'Hydrogen', 'Beyonce', 'ğŸ’¥']
        self.assertTrue(is_valid_seed(seed))

    def test_too_short(self):
        seed = ['AI', 'Zeus']
        self.assertFalse(is_valid_seed(seed))

    def test_with_duplicates(self):
        seed = ['AI', 'Zeus', 'AI', 'Gold', 'Zeus', 'ğŸ’¥']
        self.assertFalse(is_valid_seed(seed))

    def test_non_list_input(self):
        seed = "AI Zeus Venus Hydrogen Beyonce ğŸ’¥"
        self.assertFalse(is_valid_seed(seed))

    def test_empty_seed(self):
        seed = []
        self.assertFalse(is_valid_seed(seed))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    unittest.main()

3. ğŸ§¬ Seed Generator Module

seedra/core/seed_generator.py
With:
python
CopyEdit
import random
from seedra.core.categories import CATEGORIES

def generate_seed(num_words=6):
    seed = []
    used = set()
    while len(seed) < num_words:
        category = random.choice(list(CATEGORIES.keys()))
        word = random.choice(CATEGORIES[category])
        if word not in used:
            seed.append(word)
            used.add(word)
    return seed
Run it:
bash
CopyEdit
python3 -m seedra.core.seed_generator

âœ… STEP-BY-STEP: CREATE doc_gen.py

# doc_gen.py - Auto Indexing Tool for SEEDRA Modules

import os
import datetime

project_root = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
output_path = os.path.join(project_root, "seedra", "seedra_docs", "auto_doc_index.md")

header = f"""# SEEDRA MODULE INDEX

ğŸ•“ Updated: {datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()}

This document lists all key modules in the SEEDRA framework.

"""

entries = []

for root, _, files in os.walk(project_root):
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith(".py") and not file.startswith("_"):
            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, file), project_root)
            entries.append(f"- `{rel_path}`")

with open(output_path, "w") as f:
    f.write(header + "\n".join(entries))

print("âœ… `auto_doc_index.md` has been generated!")
3. Save and exit
	â€¢	Press CTRL+O to write out
	â€¢	Press Enter to confirm filename
	â€¢	Press CTRL+X to exit nano

ChatGPT said:
Yes, absolutely! Here's your polished and upgraded doc_gen.py â€” you can copy and paste this into your project at:
swift
CopyEdit
~/Downloads/OXN_PROJECT/oxnitus/seedra/doc_gen.py

python
CopyEdit
# doc_gen.py - Auto Indexing Tool for SEEDRA/OXN Modules
# ------------------------------------------------------
# ğŸ“˜ PURPOSE: Generate a symbolic, timestamped index of all .py modules
# âœï¸ Maintainer: Gonzalo Roberto Dominguez Marchan
# ğŸ“† Created: 2025-04-04
# ğŸ” Usage: Academic export, GitHub auto-doc, LaTeX conversion
# ğŸ§  Output file: docs/auto_doc_index.md

import os
import datetime

# Define base directory (adjust this path if needed)
project_root = os.path.expanduser('~/Downloads/OXN_PROJECT/oxnitus')
docs_path = os.path.join(project_root, 'docs', 'auto_doc_index.md')

# Header for index file
header = f"""# AUTO-GENERATED MODULE INDEX

This index was generated by `doc_gen.py`.

ğŸ§  Timestamp: {datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()}
ğŸ”— Project Root: {project_root}

All `.py` modules (excluding private/_ prefixed) are listed below for academic and symbolic reference.

"""

# Collect entries
entries = []
for root, dirs, files in os.walk(project_root):
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith(".py") and not file.startswith("_"):
            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, file), project_root)
            entries.append(f"- `{rel_path}`")

# Write the index
with open(docs_path, "w") as f:
    f.write(header + "\n".join(entries) + "\n")

print("âœ… doc_gen.py executed successfully.")
print(f"ğŸ“˜ Index saved to: {docs_path}")

ğŸ“Œ After saving it:
	1.	Run it with:

CopyEdit

# doc_gen.py - Auto Indexing Tool for OXN Modules
import os
import datetime

project_root = os.path.expanduser('~/Downloads/OXN_PROJECT/oxnitus')
docs_path = os.path.join(project_root, 'docs/auto_doc_index.md')

header = f"""# AUTO-GENERATED MODULE INDEX

Updated: {datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()}

"""

entries = []
for root, dirs, files in os.walk(project_root):
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith(".py") and not file.startswith("_"):
            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, file), project_root)
            entries.append(f"- `{rel_path}`")

with open(docs_path, "w") as f:
    f.write(header + "\n".join(entries))

print("ğŸ“˜ doc_gen.py completed. Index updated.")

# Symbolic Tier and Identity Registry for SEEDRA v1.0
# Author: Gonzalo Roberto Dominguez Marchan

from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from datetime import datetime

class TierRegistry:
"""
Defines symbolic access tiers for SEEDRA-based identity layers.
Tier 1: Basic (temp/rental, smart devices)
Tier 2: Personal (memory-linked, preferences, mood)
Tier 3: Root (encrypted vaults, AGI-level ops)
"""
def __init__(self):
self.tiers: Dict[int, Dict] = {
1: {"name": "Basic", "desc": "Temporary access: rentals, smart devices"},
2: {"name": "Personal", "desc": "User profile, symbolic prefs, linked memory"},
3: {"name": "Root", "desc": "Vault access, full AGI control, irreversible logs"},
}

def get_tier(self, level: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
return self.tiers.get(level, None)

def list_tiers(self) -> Dict[int, Dict]:
return self.tiers

Emoji and keyword symbolic mapping system.

# registry.py â€“ Symbolic ID Registration Tool (SEEDRA)
# Created: 2025-04-04
# Author: Gonzalo Dominguez Marchan

import random
from datetime import datetime

SYMBOLIC_VOCAB = [
    "AI", "ML", "LLM", "CV", "DL", "ETHICS", "WISDOM", "ATHENA", "MERCURY",
    "NEURAL", "DRAGONA", "PLUTO", "INTENT", "MIND", "SOMA", "TRUTH", "TOKEN",
    "NOMOS", "GAIA", "AETHER", "XENON", "EMOJI", "FIRE", "WATER", "EARTH", "AIR"
]

TIERS = {
    1: "Tier 1 - Basic",
    2: "Tier 2 - Personal",
    3: "Tier 3 - Full Access"
}

def generate_identity(seed_count=6, tier=1):
    if seed_count < 6 or seed_count > 24:
        raise ValueError("Seed count must be between 6 and 24.")
    
    identity = random.sample(SYMBOLIC_VOCAB, seed_count)
    tier_label = TIERS.get(tier, "Tier 1 - Basic")
    timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

    print("ğŸ—ï¸  New symbolic identity generated!")
    print("âœ… SEEDRA Identity:", identity)
    print("Tier:", tier_label)
    print("Timestamp:", timestamp)
    return identity

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generate_identity()
